After the Beggar Left, Armed Robbery Occurred, and the Victims Were Shot

Liu Fuxin, a 51-year-old man from Taizhou, lives in a bungalow at No. 163 Changming Road, Maigen Road, West Shanghai, with his wife, Mrs. Zhang, 43 years old, and his concubine, Mrs. Feng, 22 years old, both also from Taizhou. Liu usually makes a living by renting out rickshaws and has some savings. At around 6:50 p.m. yesterday, while Liu was having dinner with his wife and concubine, a ragged beggar came to his house to ask for help. Liu, seeing that he was pitiful, gave him two dimes. The beggar thanked him and left. Unexpectedly, as soon as the beggar reached the bamboo fence gate, four short-clad bandits suddenly jumped into the house. Two of them stood guard outside the gate empty-handed, while the other two, armed with pistols, rushed into the living room. They saw Liu's concubine, Mrs. Feng, washing the dishes, and she had a gold ring on her hand. The bandits snatched it off her finger and tried to break into the bedroom. Liu Fuxin saw this and rushed out to call for help. The two bandits heard him and quickly retreated. Seeing that Liu was still shouting, they desperately fired three or four shots and fled. Liu was shot in the right leg, and Liu's wife, Mrs. Zhang, was shot in the groin. Both fell to the ground in extreme pain. At the same time, neighbors heard the gunshots and came to investigate. Seeing the situation, they reported to the Gordon Road Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to the scene and took Liu to Bazilu Sanatorium Hospital and Liu's wife, Mrs. Zhang, to Guangren Hospital for separate treatment. Detectives were also dispatched to search for the bandits.

Case of Trafficking Women Abroad

Ning Chunda Has Sinister Intentions

Ms. Liu Gong Escapes Suspicion

Ning Chunda, a native of Hunan, 41 years old, is currently employed as a manager at Lishengxiang Boiler Factory at No. 483 Lima Road in Nanshi. Last year, Ning returned to his hometown on business and met Liu Gong, the wife of a former colleague. Ms. Liu, 26 years old, is a widow whose husband passed away and left behind a ten-year-old son. Due to the family's poverty, life has been particularly difficult since her husband's death. When Ning saw her, he was moved by her youth and beauty and tried to seduce her. He persuaded her to go to Shanghai to work in a factory. She believed him and came to Shanghai, staying at Ning's factory. After more than two months, Ning never mentioned introducing her to work at the factory. Although she repeatedly questioned him, Ning always gave vague answers. She became suspicious. The other day, Ning ordered her to go to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to obtain a passport. She thought, "Since I am not going abroad, why do I need a passport?" Fearing that Ning had ulterior motives, she refused to comply. As a result, the two sides disagreed and had a major conflict. The patrolman Wang Chunfu heard about it and brought both of them to the first district. During the preliminary interrogation, Liu Gong stated the above facts and requested an investigation. When questioned, Ning Chunda suddenly changed his story, claiming that Ms. Liu was his sister-in-law and that his brother, Chunguang, was doing business in Taiwan. She behaved improperly in the village, and last year when he returned home, she voluntarily came to Shanghai with him. The other day, he received a letter from his brother, instructing him to send her to Taiwan, so today he ordered her to go to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to obtain a passport so that she could leave for Taiwan immediately. All the things that she claimed were not true. When Liu Gong was questioned again, she said that her husband had died and that Ning intended to lure her to Taiwan and falsely claim that she was his sister-in-law. Because the statements of both parties differed, they were ordered to prepare documents and be sent to the bureau for further interrogation.

Wang Yonggao Appeals, Denying the Rape of His Adopted Daughter

The Judge Advocates for Investigating the Victim's Age

Wang Yonggao, a native of Sichuan, only 26 years old, is a cargo agent residing at Yuji Xing Zhanfang on Guangdong Road. He became acquainted with Deng Yudada, a fellow native residing in the same place. Deng had an adopted daughter, Gui Xiang, who worked as a laundress. Therefore, Wang's clothes were also given to Gui Xiang to wash, so she was able to enter and exit Wang's room frequently. In September of last year, Deng _ came to Shanghai from Sichuan and suddenly heard the tea servants of the lodge calling Gui Xiang "Mrs. Wang." He became suspicious and questioned her. Gui Xiang confessed that she had been lured and raped by Wang Yonggao on the night of September 26. Deng immediately contacted Wang, saying that he should not have raped a girl under the age of sixteen, and reported it to the General Inspectorate. Detectives were dispatched to send Gui Xiang to the hospital, where it was found that her hymen had been ruptured for a long time. Wang Yonggao was arrested and sent to the First Special District Local Court for trial. He was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment, as reported previously. Wang Yonggao was unwilling to accept the verdict and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. He stated various reasons, denying that he had committed rape, and also expressed doubt about Gui Xiang's age. He said that the claim that she was under sixteen was only stated by Deng Yuda and Gui Xiang, and there was no other definite evidence. He asked to be exonerated and the original judgment overturned. On the other hand, Deng Yuda also hired a lawyer to file a private suit against Wang Yonggao, requesting that he be ordered to pay compensation for damages. Yesterday afternoon, Court President Yu and Assessors Zhao and Zhou of the Second Branch of the High Court summoned all the witnesses to court for a hearing. In addition to stating the reasons for his objection, Wang Yonggao claimed that Gui Xiang was actually Deng's maidservant, and her appearance was not attractive. Deng wanted to give her to the tea room, but no one wanted her. How could he want to rape her? However, Gui Xiang insisted that she was summoned by Wang to the upstairs and raped. Court President Yu then questioned the witnesses who were summoned and said that the age of the victim must be verified, so he ordered that the hearing be rescheduled.

A Group of Beggars Viciously Assaulted and Killed a Man

Was He Really Killed by Falling?

Hou Ziyun, 69 years old, from Nantong, and Shen Lianfu, Zhang Hongkui, and Jin Hongkou, also from the same village, were all members of a gang of beggars. Shen rented a bungalow at No. _ Wu _ Li, Hutai Road, Zhabei, as a place for the beggars to live, and he also collected rent. Hou owed rent and did not pay, so he had an argument with Shen yesterday and they grabbed and punched each other. Hou Ziyun immediately fell to the ground, stopped breathing, and died. Zhang and Jin went to the Fourth District Police Station to report and testify. The police arrested Shen Lianfu. Shen claimed that the deceased fell down from the upstairs and died. Because the statements of the two sides differed, the order was given to take them to the science section for further interrogation, and the local official Wang Shaoting was ordered to report the case to the Local Court. Prosecutor Wu was appointed to arrive at the scene for an examination.

Xie Baofeng Became Seriously Ill in the Toilet and Died After Being Sent to the Hospital for Treatment

Autopsy Results Showed Suspicion of Poisoning

Xie Baofeng, also known as _ Yi, 28 years old, from Suzhou, was a silk merchant in his hometown. Recently, he had _ to go to Shaoxing. The hospital reported it to the Old Gate Police Station, who ordered detectives to investigate. The body was then taken to the forensic examination office on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Local Court was requested to appoint Prosecutor _ Yaoguang to arrive at the scene to examine the body. He ascended to the official seat and questioned Xie's father, _ Yun _, who _ to _, living in Suzhou. He said, "Last night, I learned about it through a _ report from the hotel, so I rushed here to collect the body. My son went to Shaoxing to sweep the tomb this time. He was not ill when he left, and he was very frugal on weekdays. Now that he has died, I request that an autopsy be waived." The tea servant Ma Fuhai also gave a statement about the circumstances at the time. The body was handed over to his father, Xie Yunbao, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial."

Records of the Interrogation of the Bandits in the Kidnapping Case of Wang Zilin's Young Son

A Date Is Set for the Announcement of the Judgment After the Hearing

Wang Zilin, a native of Weihaiwei, residing at No. 722 Weihaiwei Road, is a leader in the Shanghai Municipal Council and has a comfortable family life. His four-year-old son, Fuhai, is lively and cute, and Wang cherishes him like a pearl. Unexpectedly, at 5:45 a.m. on the seventh morning of the fourth lunar month of last year, several kidnappers broke in, went upstairs, and kidnapped Fuhai. They also shot and killed the concubine Li Tao, and Wang Zilin was also shot in the leg. Later, the gang sent a letter demanding a large ransom. The location was in Haimen Township. Wang had no choice but to pay 10,000 yuan to buy Fuhai back. Later, the detectives of the Hongkou Police Station, Bao Shuji and Wang Zhusheng, the detective chief Shi Enjian, and the detectives of the Yangshupu Police Station successively arrested the kidnappers from Yancheng, Wang Xiaosizi Jiang Shihua, Fang Shulin, and fourteen others, and sent them to the First Special District Court. Those who were found to be unrelated were released. Wang and the other three were re-examined by the adjudicator Wu Ze _ yesterday afternoon. The lawyer for the police station, Zhang Tianyin, said that the police station was prosecuting the three defendants in accordance with Article 1, Section 1, and Article 285, Section 1, of the Law on Punishing Bandits for murder, and Section 2 for attempted murder. Wang Xiaosizi Jiang Shihua and others had completely confessed to the charges at the police station and accompanied the detectives to the victim's house to demonstrate the various circumstances of the kidnapping, and the blue car was parked on the east side of the Yongqingli intersection. The car belonged to a Zhao, residing at No. 65 Aivenyi Road. When the police detectives went to arrest him, he had already fled without a trace. Now the second landlord of the house can testify to this, and he has also identified the leaders Jin Rubiyi Yuting, and the accomplices surnamed Yan, Yang, Agen, and Yan's wife also went together. However, Fang Shulin and the two defendants, Wang and Jiang, were taken there by two faction leaders and did not know each other. Before the incident, at around 7:00 p.m. on April 25, Jin and Bi _ led them to hold a joint meeting in Room 8 of the Zhongnan Hotel at No. 345 Mintiniying Road in the French Concession. Afterwards, the two defendants, Wang and Jiang, each received 240 yuan, and Fang received 50 yuan. However, he was arrested by the Yangshupu Police Station for another case and confessed to the case. All the confessions related to this case are the same as the confessions made by the two defendants, Wang and Jiang, at the Hongkou Police Station. The victim was present and understood the confessions when the three defendants were recording their confessions at the police station, and he is also present in court today. Wang Zilin and his lawyer, Zhou Xiaoan, stated that the bandits entered while the maid Li Tao was emptying the chamber pot. The young son Fuhai was sleeping with his mother-in-law in the adjacent room upstairs. One bandit went upstairs, took the child from the bed and carried him downstairs, and the mother-in-law warned him. He got up and went downstairs.

He saw two bandits taking out guns and threatening them to remain silent. The maid was shot and killed for looking around. His leg was also shot. The child was carried out of the back door by the bandits. Later, the three defendants admitted their confessions at the police station. He understood clearly, but at the time he was frightened and could not identify the faces of the bandits. His words still showed fear and his sentences trembled. Lawyer Zhou Chen substituted. According to Lu Jincai, who lived at No. 65 Aivenyi Road, _ the landlord, there was indeed a tenant surnamed Zhao living there, and there was a blue-topped car, which was often parked in the back door. It was said that the car was for hiring customers to ride in. He had a wife and two children. During the third month of the lunar calendar last year, they suddenly moved to another place. When questioned, the three defendants, Wang and others, completely overturned their police confessions and previous admissions in court. The court read out the previous confessions in detail, questioned them strictly for a long time, put forward key points, and criticized them for being cunning, but one defendant still stammered. After the presiding judge Wu appointed a lawyer to defend the defendants and the police lawyer, he ordered the three defendants to be returned to custody and a date was set for the announcement of the judgment.

Shanghai Post Office News The airmail postage rate has been increased from 1.5 cents to 2.5 cents for every 20 grams or fraction thereof within each flight zone. All airmail letters with insufficient postage, in addition to requiring double payment of the deficiency, may be delayed as a result.

Report on Reserve Funds Issued by Four Banks

No. 161

The Four Banks Reserve Fund is jointly established by the Yien Yieh, Kincheng, China & South Sea, and Continental Banks, and specializes in the issuance of banknotes by China & South Sea Bank. According to the issuance regulations of the fund, the issuance of banknotes is fully backed by reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guarantee reserves accounting for up to 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and it is audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. Reader's Advisor

Problem of Changing Professions (1)

| Letter from Mr. Wu |

I am a young man with weak will and lacking in ability. Because I want to solve my livelihood problem, when I was fifteen years old, I abandoned what I liked and left my hometown for a shop in a town thousands of miles away to become an apprentice! Of course, I have great hopes for my career. I want to struggle through my apprenticeship! Every day I do some sweeping work, which is of course the hardship that we young people should endure. I want to steal a little free time from these tasks to learn writing and abacus skills, which are essential in the business world. However, reality does not allow you to do this! Now, my three-year apprenticeship is over, and the resulting price is that my back is injured from carrying heavy objects. Now I think, I wanted to learn all the knowledge of business, so why didn't he allow me to? If he doesn't allow me, then don't I have no job? Then isn't my time wasted in vain? I have no knowledge at all, where in society is there a place for me to stand? I think that if I continue to learn like this, even if I learn until old age, wouldn't I still be the same as before? Rather than that, I think it's better to change careers early. But I don't have any knowledge of other careers. I think I can work as a tea server, and I can still get a little salary every month to support my family. I am writing to ask for your guidance, do you think my plan is good?

Answer: Apprentices in the old days didn't learn much, except to be slaves to the shop owner and senior staff. This was the common situation. As for writing and abacus skills, they all depended on the apprentice's own "seeing and feeling," flattering an accountant or clerk, and asking them to teach them in their spare time, in order to have a chance to gain some skills. If you think you are learning business and are waiting for the shop owner or the shop staff to automatically teach you, then you have made a mistake. You may have suffered a loss because of this. If you want to earn a few coins immediately to "support your family," it may be okay to change careers to be a tea server, if the tea server can earn a few coins more than a newly graduated apprentice. As for learning, that is another issue. However, the tea server may be a little more relaxed than the apprentice, and may be able to steal some time to study, which is unknown, and it depends on how much you struggle.

Educational News

Important News

Shandong Department of Education Orders Schools to Strictly Enforce Examinations

(Jinan, February 11th) The Shandong Department of Education, noting that in the recent middle school graduation examinations, many students had four or five subjects failing, or all subjects failing, has specifically ordered all public and private middle schools in the province to strictly enforce examinations for students in their daily work, in accordance with departmental regulations.

Informal Discussion on Educational Inspection in the Capital by Ministry of Education Personnel

The Ministry of Education previously sent secretaries, counselors, supervisors, and others to jointly inspect national, provincial, and municipal primary and secondary schools and social education institutions, as well as private primary and secondary schools, in the capital for a period of three months. The work has now been completed. Yesterday, a reporter interviewed the inspection personnel. According to them, a total of 30 secondary schools were inspected (schools for the descendants of martyrs, the Central University Experimental School, provincial, municipal, and private middle schools), more than 70 public and private primary schools, more than 10 public and private kindergartens, several social education institutions, and several private schools.

Financial Aspects

In addition to the national Central University, provincial and municipal middle schools and schools for the descendants of martyrs have a total of more than 370,000 yuan, private middle schools have more than 560,000 yuan, including more than 60,000 yuan in subsidies, provincial and municipal primary schools have more than 690,000 yuan, and private primary schools have about 100,000 yuan, including more than 30,000 yuan in subsidies. Compared with the statistics before 1927, there has been rapid progress. However, the city lacks a foundation. The municipal government has established a foundation committee. In accordance with Chairman Dai Jitao's plan to raise funds, the current national crisis makes it difficult to achieve the desired results, and alternative sources of funding must be found. The city of Beijing originally had a plan to add 25 schools, but due to school building problems, difficulty in finding land, and a lack of construction funds, it is better to expand the existing schools' grades. It is heard that more than ten grades have already been added.

Student Aspects

Muscles are underdeveloped, physical education is insufficient, trachoma accounts for 70-80%, and the number of skin diseases is also alarming. Therefore, school physical education should be given special attention.

School Aspects

Principals are able to work hard in handling school affairs, and generally do a good job. However, there are too many meetings in municipal schools. It is advisable to reduce formal meetings and hold simple discussion meetings to save time and engage in practical work. Teachers have very few opportunities for further study at school. The municipal bureau should take advantage of the time and hold training courses for schools in different districts, once every week or two, for one or two hours each time.

Equipment Aspects

Most municipal schools lack adequate scientific equipment. It is best for the municipal bureau to set up a central manufacturing plant in cooperation with vocational schools, or to convert vocational schools into mechanical and woodworking departments to manufacture scientific instruments and desks and chairs for the use of various schools, thus avoiding the exclusive purchase of foreign goods, so that the rights and interests will not flow out. And vocational education is more likely to be effective in adapting to the needs of training. Also, principals should use more of their administrative office expenses to purchase specimens and scientific equipment and supplies, and buy less unnecessary items, so that over the years, the equipment will be considerable. According to the management of educational undertakings, qualifications, knowledge, experience, and service interests must all be given equal importance, especially the professional spirit. The municipal bureau should strive for prudence in the initial selection of principals. After taking office, there should not be many changes, so that the educational spirit is consistent, and efforts should be made to avoid reducing efficiency. A small number of schools hire students who are still studying in universities or middle schools as class teachers. Class teachers have many tasks and responsibilities. Even taking on extra classes is considered to be distracting, and studying at the same time is bound to be difficult. It would be less of a problem if these teachers were changed to teaching specialized subjects. As for the teachers of each school, there is no obvious lack in teaching and guidance, but private middle schools have overcrowded school buildings and a great lack of equipment, and should strive to improve. It is also heard that this inspection will not make many negative criticisms, but will provide positive guidance.

Five external medical assistants; (11) Nineteen students have won special awards from various institutions and schools. Local.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Regularly Inspects the Physical Fitness of Students in Various Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education yesterday instructed the municipal primary and secondary schools in the South Shanghai, North Gate, and Gaoqiao districts: "Investigating student physical fitness is one of the central plans for health education. The Bureau of Health has already sent personnel to conduct inspections in the last semester. To continue this work, a list of physical fitness inspections for municipal schools in the South Shanghai, Zhabei, and Gaoqiao districts has been drawn up and distributed to each school. At the appointed time, each school shall appoint one or two faculty members to earnestly assist in the process and record the necessary information. A documentary film has been prepared and each school is required to send someone to the Bureau of Health's health office beforehand to pick it up and utilize it. Please comply with this order." Attached are copies of the lists of physical fitness inspections for municipal schools in the South Shanghai and Zhabei districts, and the list of physical fitness inspections for municipal schools in the Gaoqiao district (lists omitted).

Results of the Shanghai Municipal Council Middle School Scholarship Examination Announced

The Shanghai Municipal Council previously decided to establish ten scholarships in the Council's Chinese and general middle schools, with the scholarship amount being half of the annual tuition fee. Among them, four scholarships are for boys from the Council's primary schools, four scholarships are for boys from non-Council primary schools, and two scholarships are for girls from the Council's primary schools. The results of the recent examination have been announced. A total of 42 candidates took the test, all of whom were boys because there were no qualified girls. The subjects of the examination were Chinese language, history, geography, nature, English, and arithmetic. The following candidates have now been selected to receive scholarships: Chen Nian and Guo (both students of the North District Primary School), and who will be admitted to the Shanghai Chinese Public School; Gui Shiji and Xu Shang (both students of the East District Primary School), and will be admitted to the Nie Zhongcheng Public School. In addition, Chen Yaoxing (North District Primary School) and Zhou Qinzhang (East District Primary School) will be alternates. Among the non-Council primary school students who participated in the examination, Guan Yanlou and Han Dong (both from the Suzhou Shanghai Hostel Primary School) will be admitted to the Gezhi Public School; Ma Fangcui (Wenwei Primary School) and Wang Lingen (Jing'an Primary School) will be admitted to the Yucai Public School. In addition, Yang Chunsheng (Wenwei Primary School) and Chen Bonian (Binhai Primary School) will be alternates. All those admitted will receive a scholarship. If those admitted are unable to attend the designated school, the alternate candidates will be moved up. The following students also took the examination and had excellent results: Meng Jiren (North District), Huang Defu (East District), Li Yuting (East District), Cao Yuchang (East District), Chen Qizhan (North District), Cai Xieheng, Qiu Jinshan, Zhang Xinbao (all from the East District), Mao Demei Chen Tong (both from the North District), Yan Ji (Binhai), Zhu Jinyuan (Jing'an).

City Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan's Speech "Shanghai's Education (3)"

Overview of School Education and Social Education

(4) Normal Schools: In recent years, the number of primary schools in this city has gradually increased, and there is a great shortage of teachers, especially kindergarten and rural primary school teachers. Therefore, in 1929, a private kindergarten normal school was added, and in the academic year of 1930, a municipal rural normal school was founded. In total, the number of normal schools in the 1931-1932 academic year was one municipal school and eight private schools, totaling nine schools. The required funding was 155,879 yuan, of which the municipal normal school's funding accounted for 14,495 yuan. The number of students was 1,286, and the number of teachers was 187, naturally including staff. The equipment is similar to that of middle schools, so it will not be described in detail.

(5) Vocational Schools: In this city, the national vocational schools include only the National Tongji University Affiliated Mechanic School. The ministry-run schools include the Ministry of Communications-run Telecommunications School. Private schools include the Private China Vocational Middle School, Private Tongde Midwifery School, Private Zhongde Midwifery School, and Private Renhe Midwifery School, etc. The funding for the China Vocational School is the largest, about 78,580 yuan. The statistical report of vocational schools for the 1931-1932 academic year is as follows:

Number of Schools Number of Students Number of Faculty and Staff Amount of Funding

National 1 59 29

Ministry 1 6 25 18,000

Provincial 1 116 25 9,96

Private Registered 5 1,488 146 170,38

Private Unregistered 2 97 45 40,671

Total 2 1,746 270 288,975

(6) Municipal Higher Education: Higher education is talent education. If there are only primary and secondary schools but no universities, it only provides ordinary training and civic training for the general public, but lacks talent cultivation and leadership training. Shanghai has a population of 3.5 million, so primary schools must be expanded as much as possible. With the expansion of primary schools, secondary schools and normal schools must also be promoted as much as possible. However, for the purpose of cultivating talents for the country and creating leaders for society, higher education should also have the same development. Higher education in this city includes specialized schools, independent colleges, and universities. Although it is still far from our goal, it is considered to be progressing relatively quickly among the major cities in the country. However, we feel that there are too many universities and colleges in Shanghai, and the establishment of departments and faculties is somewhat duplicated, which is really uneconomical. We will now give a brief overview due to time constraints:

(A) Specialized Schools: There is one national specialized school in this city, with a total of 127 students, 24 faculty and staff, and funding of approximately 126,339 yuan. There are two ministry-run specialized schools in this city, with a total of 230 students, 49 faculty and staff, and a total annual funding of 162,000 yuan. There is one private registered specialized school in this city, with a total of 1,027 students, 178 faculty and staff, and an annual funding of over 100,000 yuan.

(B) Independent Colleges: There are three national independent colleges in this city, with a total of 271 students, 132 faculty and staff, and an annual funding of over 399,000 yuan. As for private registered independent colleges, there are four, with a total of 2,538 students, 217 faculty and staff, and a total annual funding of over 367,000 yuan. There are also seven private unregistered colleges, with a total of 1,623 students, 9 faculty and staff, and an annual funding of over 176,000 yuan.

(C) Universities: There are four national universities in this city, with a total of 1,752 students, 436 faculty and staff, and a total annual funding of over 1,415,000 yuan. There are six private registered universities in this city, with a total of 717 students, 703 faculty and staff, and a total annual funding of over 1,641,000 yuan. There are three private unregistered universities, with a total of 642 students, 163 faculty and staff, and a total annual funding of approximately 605,000 yuan.

(7) Municipal Science Laboratory: Due to economic limitations, the municipal primary schools in this city are naturally unable to have fully complete equipment for natural sciences. However, given China's underdeveloped material resources and the lack of popularity of natural sciences, if we want to promote science education, the departmental equipment of each school must be expanded. Therefore, the Municipal Education Bureau has specially established a municipal science laboratory to purchase specimens and machines so that students from all municipal primary schools can have the opportunity to conduct experiments.

The above is a general description of school education. Now, let's talk about social education.

In this city, we must know that it is much more difficult and arduous to work hard in the field of social education than in the field of school education. First, social education is multi-faceted and it is not easy to concentrate efforts. Second, social education is widespread, and it is not easy to popularize efforts. Third, there are many reactionary forces in social education, making it difficult to maintain its comprehensive efficiency. Fourth, invisible and inappropriate social forces are spreading everywhere due to the complexity of the social environment, making it difficult for well-regulated and good social education to have lasting effects.

Although our efforts may not achieve the results we desire, in any case, in order to ensure that all aspects of society receive a well-regulated and good amount of social education, whether in the active or passive aspects, we have considerable plans and facilities. Naturally, we cannot help but feel the lack of funds, the shortage of talent, and the incompleteness of plans and facilities. However, within the possible scope, we are confident that we have made considerable progress in the necessary work that should be done in recent years.

Next, Vice President Wang Jiyuan reported on the recent art movements in the world and in China, as well as the school's new facilities in the future, and encouraged the students to strive for practical work and diligent study in order to save the country from its difficulties. Director Zhang of the Academic Affairs Department reported on the reforms in academic affairs and the addition of painters who have returned from Europe, such as Kang, as professors of Western painting. The ceremony ended at 12:00 noon. It was also reported that the school is scheduled to officially start classes on the 16th. There are still vacancies available in each department and for transfer students. Those who are interested can register for the entrance examination at any time.

Order to Abolish the National Games Preparatory Committee

To be Taken Over by the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum Management Committee

Random Thoughts

Adana Models Paraded in the Streets

— Zhanlu

This joke is really something: In the women's bathhouse in Adana, Turkey, because someone spread rumors about the building collapsing, many female bathers were so frightened that they staged a funny scene of models parading in the streets. Reuters teletype spread the news to countries around the world. This is not only a mockery of the world, but simply a laughingstock of the world.

I remember that last year, there was a fire in a bathhouse in Nanjing, and it seemed that there was also a funny scene of male models parading in the streets. However, this was a local joke, and Reuters teletype did not spread the news to countries around the world. Both are model parades. Why does the female parade have the value of being spread by Reuters to countries around the world? This is a very interesting question, perhaps containing some philosophy of life and social psychology?

The rumor-monger was a female bather. She tricked the other female bathers into running away without taking their personal protective items. She then unceremoniously swept away everyone's clothes and fled. Everyone said she was playing a prank, but I say: She is not playing a prank, she is the commander of the total mobilization of laughter for countries around the world!

Turkish-style bathing is very fashionable in Shanghai, and it also has a long history in Europe. Last year, Dr. Huijin, director of the British Museum in London, discovered the bathrooms of the Roman Empire more than 1,700 years ago during archaeological excavations. There were complete hot air pipes leading to the walls, and the interior layout and Turkish-style bathroom equipment were similar. This shows the long history of Turkish-style bathing. However, in this long "bathing history" of more than 1,700 years, it is probably not easy to find a similar scene of female models parading in the streets.

This is a once-in-a-millennium funny scene, so it has the value of being spread by Reuters to countries around the world.

The Gravitational Pull of the Earth

— Xu Jie

From the perspective of "quantity," people are most unequal: Bank bosses print out countless colorful banknotes, build Western-style houses, ride in automobiles, take concubines, order people around with arrogance, and command respect. Even their farts are complimented as fragrant. Rickshaw pullers brave wind and snow, pulling people around all day long, yet they can't earn even a dime or two. They might even be rewarded with a few slaps by the police, which is a common occurrence. Then there are the laborers who climb to the tops of ten-story buildings for a few dimes in wages; if they're not careful and fall, turning into mincemeat, their deaths go unavenged. Architects, however, merely talk and point, designing blueprints, seemingly unconcerned about the sacrifices of these laborers. As for writers, they rack their brains and pour out their heart's blood, becoming severely neurasthenic, writing at most four to five thousand words every two days and receiving twenty to thirty yuan in compensation. Ultimately, they keep writing day after day, shortening their lifespans. Yet, plump capitalists can effortlessly gain ten or a hundred thousand with a phone call or a verbal command. From the perspective of "quantity," are people truly equal?

Nowadays, people believe in Einstein's theory of relativity and no longer believe in Newton's theory of gravity. From the perspective of the current state of society, Einstein's theory of relativity naturally holds sway. However, Newton's theory of gravity is indeed an eternal truth that cannot be broken. For example, we struggle for food and clothing, toiling our entire lives just to avoid hunger and cold. This is called "struggling to death." But even wealthy people with plenty of food and clothing only eat three meals a day and sleep one night. Although they don't have to live like beasts of burden, they can live a comfortable "pig-like life." This is called "waiting to die," and the outcome is no different from ours. Who doesn't know that Tao Zhu, Yi Dun, Deng Tong, and Shi Chong were wealthy men? But today, who among them hasn't been pulled into the earth by gravity, becoming a mound of yellow earth, forever sleeping? Alas! Newton's theory can be said to be "the most equal axiom."

Shanghai Night Talk: The Greatness of the "Little Man" (Illustration)

— Xianxian

After dinner, chatting with friends to kill time is too boring. Flipping through the works of great writers that I bought but haven't read requires sharpening a knife before cutting and reading, which is too much trouble. Stretching and yawning, preparing to sleep, I'm afraid of indigestion and think of castor oil. Neither left nor right works, so I decide to take a stroll on the road and appreciate the greatness of the urban night.

Strange, in less than three minutes, the customers have already covered a table with colorful banknotes. Being so generous and throwing money away, if someone went to donate to disaster relief, there would be no shortage of hope. Great is the generosity of gamblers.

On the Way to Chuansha

— Huoxueming

The municipal ferry, like a giant sea turtle, belching black smoke, cuts through the yellow and沉沉 waves, striving to leave the Bund, carrying my heart and shooting like an arrow towards the eastern shore.

The fresh air and warm breeze on the water envelop the boat. Leaning against the railing, I watch the silver waves, the giant buildings of the city, the bustling crowds, and the smoke billowing from the red chimneys on the plains. I realize that the world is constantly in turmoil, and all life is breathing.

Green trees and crops are full of spring smiles. People's cheeks are reddened by the sunlight, singing in the social groups. Even if it's a song of sorrow and pain, this sorrow and pain is a treasure of life, and I will never give it up.

Soon, the red walls of "Qingning Temple" jumped into view. Disembarking from the boat, I quickly boarded a small light train, rolling forward on the scattered stone tracks. Like a camel, the train carried us as we leisurely viewed the rural scenery: oxen sleeping in the grass, white sheep scattered in the fields, children riding on dogs, geese and ducks floating on the water...

Getting off at "Muzi Bridge," I switched to a small fishing boat to visit a friend. The sound of oars entered the reed flower harbor, and a deep river stretched before me. Suddenly, a small boat flew past, the red shirts of the village girls reflected on the emerald green spring water, so bright, so beautiful, yet fleeting so quickly.

Under the dim streetlights, I looked out at the sidewalks, filled with living model girls dressed in red silk and green brocade.

Strangely, these enchanting and charming girls are said to have transformed into "wild chickens" in the eyes of Shanghainese men. It is said that these wild chickens are the great benefactors of venereal disease doctors, because they mysteriously cultivate venereal disease seeds on the bodies of "wild chicken hunters," like farmers cultivating excellent fruits, so that "wild chicken hunters" naturally take care of the venereal disease doctors' wealth. Logically speaking, "wild chicken hunters," whose bodies and hair are received from their parents, should not generously allow the wild chickens to experiment with venereal disease seed cultivation. However, the fact that the sidewalks are full of living model girls proves the large number of "wild chicken hunters" who are willing to sacrifice everything. Great is the spirit of the "wild chicken hunter."

As I was admiring the greatness of the "wild chicken hunter's" spirit, nodding and sighing with emotion, I met an old friend whom I hadn't seen in a long time. He took me to a gambling den at "Number 217," which was neither too big nor too small. I squeezed through the gamblers and glanced at the table, only to see colorful banknotes piled up. A burst of shouts and cheers swept away the clouds, and the winnings went into the pockets of the gambling den owner. It was so lively...

Then came the silent, lonely village, and the faint chirping of nameless birds in the cypress forest, crisp and melodious. Letting the sound of the oars stop, the fishing boat drifted in the middle of the river. The sun was warm, the wind was gentle, and the world was so peaceful. By the time we reached Chuansha City, it was already dusk.

Fiction

Photograph

— Mo Yi

"He's dead, how could there be so much blood if he wasn't dead?"

"That's right. This guy is definitely dead... Haha, you guys want to be fierce, huh? You were so powerful the night before, what's wrong today?... We didn't even use much effort, just a small trick, and we sent you all to your ancestors'... Haha, when you get to the underworld, tell the volunteer soldiers who paved the way in detail... Haha..." The enemy, laughing and speaking, kicked Zhang Rongji's head hard twice, and he immediately fainted.

At this time, the snow was falling harder and harder than before, and the roaring wind was blowing even stronger. The snow fell on the fresh blood, turning into red snow. But soon, the bright red blood was all covered by the white snow, and there was no trace of blood on the ground, as if there had never been a massacre, a major bloodshed here. Zhang Rongji was slowly awakened by the wind. He could no longer hear any human voices except for the whistling wind. He secretly raised his head, glanced around, and knew that the cruel executioners were all gone. He slowly struggled to get up, his head still throbbing with pain. He staggered and moved his limbs, lowered his head, and looked at the corpses with their brains split open and their flesh and blood blurred, lying all over the ground. He couldn't help but be shocked and cried like a madman, running wildly around the mountain like a fool. After running around for a while, he suddenly smelled the burnt smell of something burning. He stopped and took a closer look, realizing that he had run to the village of Pingdingshan, but the houses in the entire village had already been burned, with only embers still burning. He raised his head again and looked towards Qianjinbao and Lizigou Village: in the hazy mist, the raging fire rolled in the strong wind, as if the afterglow of the setting sun reflected the surrounding woods... (The End)

Shanghai Night Talk

— Zhang Ruo

The Little Man

After watching "Good Night, Vienna" at the Nanjing Grand Theatre, the electric lights on Edward VII Avenue shone like daylight. Those strings of three-lamp lampstands, hanging in the sky like the Chinese character 川, were an artificial white rainbow of tens of thousands of candles, illuminating this ever-bright city's grand avenue. How worthy of praise is the night of Shanghai!

I walked alone on the sidewalk, my ears not retaining the melody of the "Good Night, Vienna" song, my mind still filled with the images of laughter and song, wine and women. I had dreamed of Vienna, that "city of laughter and love, a paradise full of romantic atmosphere," for ten years. On the silver screen, I had satisfied my spiritual travels once.

Arriving at the most magnificent area of the French Concession, that area where three model streets converged in a 工-shape; the two horizontal and parallel Avenues Joffre and Route Pichon resembled the Chinese character "二," and the vertical Avenue Amiral Courbet in the middle resembled the 丨-stroke. These three roads commemorating great generals, great lawyers, and great archbishops were truly good places for pedestrians to take a stroll!

Several dozen "Silver Dragons" and "Renault" brand cars, large and small, were parked in front of the French Club, which looked like ivory or a palace of the Jade Emperor. Inside the revolving door, the back of a French girl disappeared. In front of the fourteen-story skyscraper-like building, a tall and long-bodied White Russian gatekeeper paced back and forth in front of the Cathay Apartments, bored to death. In front of the Lyceum Theatre and the Cathay Theatre, the red and green neon lights dazzled the eyes. The 5:30 show had just ended, and the 9:15 late show had not yet started. Not a single man or woman was to be seen, only the portrait of Greta Garbo with long eyelashes on the advertisement, a seductive facial expression that made one's heart flutter.

Across from the tennis lawn on Avenue Joffre, a café had the German words "Little Man" written on its large glass window. Feeling the need to rest, I pushed the door open and went in.

The coffee seats were arranged in a very modern style. Sitting in the semi-circular leather armchair felt extraordinarily comfortable and pleasant. The walls were lit with golden lights. A tall and slender girl, dressed like a alabaster statue, came over to greet me. I casually ordered a cup of coffee.

"Are you from Vienna?" Because I saw the "Little Man's" decoration, which had a Viennese flavor, I asked her this question in German when the waitress brought the coffee pot and cup.

She smiled and replied in German, "I am from Berlin."

My knowledge of German is very limited. Although I recently met a young man from Vienna, Professor Luo Yimin, who now teaches German at Jiaotong University, he is fluent in Chinese. When we meet, we both speak Chinese. This young professor from Austria, although he grew up in Vienna, doesn't have a fluent Beijing accent. I haven't had the opportunity to learn German with him, so I have things to say in my heart, but I can't say them with my mouth. I have no way to communicate with that waitress from Berlin.

That Greek statue-like waitress wore a coffee-colored woolen robe, her brown-yellow hair combed neatly, her serene expression like a classical sculpture. She sat silently by the counter, one of her fair and clean hands supporting her chin, looking at the beautiful candy boxes in the glass cabinet, lost in thought. Looking at a beauty under the lights is such a poetic and serene picture!

The radio was broadcasting a Viennese song from "Congress Dances": "It's a pity it's only such a today; it will never be encountered again in the future! This ideal reality is too noble! Like a golden light in the heavenly palace..."

I sat alone in the "Little Man's" leather armchair, feeling both lonely and bored. I paid the bill, and as I walked out the door, the waitress from Berlin said "Thank you" in French, MERCI. I also replied to her in French, "Good night, goodbye," BON SOIR, AU REVOIR.

The Paris Theatre was showing "The Congress Dances." I spent another two hours of the lovely Shanghai night in the dark world.

Vienna and wine: laughter and singing: Shanghai and movies: coffee and waitresses: this is the nightlife of a big city!

Money Market Officially Opens Afternoon Session

Li Split early and noon are identical... Copper coins contract wind more often

A Glimpse of the Market

Since the opening of the money market at the beginning of the lunar new year, only the morning session has been conducted, and the afternoon session trading has been temporarily suspended. This was originally a common practice every year. This year, due to the inconvenience of buying and selling by the banks, the afternoon session was opened earlier after the Lantern Festival. In fact, the market has not yet been activated, and the use of silver dollars is still in a state of quietness. Because there is no need to open the session, although the afternoon session trading has already started yesterday, the trading situation is not as prosperous as the morning session in a single day. From this, we can see the approximate bleakness of the recent market.

Li Split Same Price

Because there were few transactions in the "Foreign Li" morning session and no competition, the resulting Li price was similar to the previous day, slightly better by 1 hao 2 hu and a half, settling at 7 qian 1 fen 4 li 6 hao 2 hu and a half. Unexpectedly, there were even fewer transactions in the afternoon session and even less competition, resulting in no change in the Li price, remaining the same as the morning session at 7 qian 1 fen 4 li 6 hao 2 hu and a half. Both the morning and afternoon sessions of "Silver Split" opened with white lending. The looseness of the silver market and the scarcity of its use are unprecedented facts of the year's slack season. The head drawings are also drawn in white.

Copper Coin Heavy Currency

The currency market saw Jiangnan small foreign coins rise early and weaken in the afternoon. The morning session saw 8,000 jiao transactions, and the afternoon session saw 2,000 jiao. The Guangdong small foreign coins fluctuated only slightly, rising and falling by only 3 hao and a half. The morning session was 5 qian fen 1 li and a half, and the afternoon session was 5 qian 9 fen 1 li and 7 hao and a half. Copper coins inexplicably contracted, and even severely. The difference between the two sessions was as much as 8,000 wen. Yesterday, it contracted again by 4,500 wen, to 414,000 wen, with 45,600 strings of wen traded.

Silver Dollars Calm

The amount of "Silver Funds" collected yesterday was probably better than in the past. Yarn and Cotton

Plain Yarn and Cotton, No Special Features

Since the first half of the new year, yarn sales have not been active in any state. The daily turnover in the market is only about three or four hundred bales. This situation is rare in the past, which shows the decline of domestic commerce and the difficulties of farmers' livelihoods. As for the Cantonese help, the largest consumer of Chinese yarn in Nanbu, they suffered heavy losses last year and have not yet cleared up. The financial situation is extremely tight, so the current intake is quite stagnant. After the war in Sichuan, the local area is devastated, and inferior yarn from the Yangtze River occupies the market. The shipment of local yarn from North China to Shanghai is still uninterrupted. All these situations are unfavorable to yarn sales. The future market price may be difficult to establish.

Manbiao Fluctuations Very Slight

At the opening of the Manbiao morning market, the rise in foreign cotton slightly boosted morale. Scattered shorts covered, and each month rose by three or four qian. In the second and third rounds, it was heard that the actual demand was not good, and then it weakened again. As a result, the near months rose by two or three qian, and the far months fell by one or two qian. The market atmosphere was still weak in the afternoon, with the near months falling by two qian and the far months rising by one, two, or three qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 21,800 bales. It was found that Changfeng sold 1,700 bales, Xinhua 500 bales, Chunjie 700 bales, Feng 500 bales, Renfeng 450 bales, and Tongji 400 bales. Jifeng bought 1,250 bales, Hengyi 800 bales, Mingde 850 bales, Ruida 500 bales, Zhenji 400 bales, and Yichang 400 bales. The closing prices are as follows,

Yarn Sales As Numb As Before

The removal of existing yarn remains sluggish. It was found that the total number of bales purchased by various gangs throughout the day was 448 bales. Prices fell by five qian to one liang. The purchase amount of each gang is as follows:

Shantou 45 Tianjin 5 Fujian 10 Guangdong 162

Inland 99 Xiamen 1 Fellow traders 73

The situation in the cotton market is slightly stable, but the situation is still weak. Because the overseas cotton market is still flat, but gold prices are firm, the morale of the longs is more stable, and the amount absorbed by most cotton merchants in the long position remains unchanged. However, the demand for spot cotton is still weak. The factories believe that the world cotton industry is still in an era of excess and that foreign cotton still has the hope of falling, so they are very slack about kapok.

Zheng Biao's Rising Power is Weak

At the opening of the Zheng Biao morning market, the slight rise in foreign cotton caused scattered shorts to cover and longs to buy, and the market became more firm. Each month rose by two and a half qian. In the second and third rounds, it fell again due to selling pressure. As a result, it rose by five fen to one qian. In the afternoon, it rose again by five fen to one qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 42,500 dan. It was found that Yifeng sold 3,600 dan, Xiesheng 1,000 dan, Yuanda 2,300 dan, Yicheng 1,100 dan, Shenji 1,700 dan, Renfeng 1,200 dan, Suilong 1,600 dan, and Yukang 2,200 dan. Cotton Scattered and Almost Exhausted

Spot cotton business is completely stagnant, and yarn sales are even more sluggish. There is absolutely no intention to buy high-priced cotton, so the daily clearance of transactions can be described as follows.

Overseas Cotton Telegrams Show Upward Trend

Yesterday, the US cotton market was strong and active due to the good cloth market and enthusiastic buyers. Later, it weakened due to some longs taking profits. Futures rose by three to six pounds, and spot rose by ten pounds. British cotton futures rose by four points, and spot rose by two points. Egyptian cotton spot rose by four points. Indian cotton shorts covered, and the market was tight and stable. Pingguoer rose by two rupees, Omra rose by 2.25 rupees, and Bairuoxi rose by 1.5 rupees. Grain Glutinous Rice Outdated, Both Fell by Half a Yuan

Du Geng, Ke Xian, Sales Stagnant and Weak

(South Shanghai) Yesterday's source was more than 40 ships, and the accumulation in Pudong was still acceptable. The merchants were quite willing to sell. However, since Shanghai complied with the Shanghai Dou Standards, which was put into effect on February 1st, it has been more than a week. Yesterday, some merchants suddenly used six-dou Shanghai Standards, which caused panic among boatmen, who rejected the Shanghai Standard one after another, resulting in the stagnation of retail buyers' intake. As a result, the market fell. Changxiang, Su Tong, South Port, Qingjiao, and other rice, as well as Du Yangjian, fell by one or two jiao. Bianyuan was out of season, and the taste was bland, with the price reduced by half a yuan. Yinyuan was short of goods and tasted fragrant, and the price could still stand. Factories sold Yin Bianyuan, Ke Yuan, Ke Jian, Jian, Xijian, Kun Geng, and other rice. The market was not very different.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, more than 30 ships arrived from various gangs in Hexia. White Geng shops sold slightly at lower prices, and the market was slightly angled. The arrival of thin rice was few, and retail was not bad. The arrival of early rice was not prosperous, and sales were absolutely flat. The market was sluggish. Sheep tip arrivals were continuous, and retail was slow, with a slight decrease of one or two jiao. Du Pu's arrival was low and sales were flat, with a slight drop in price. Ke Jian was also sluggish and weak. Yinyuan was short of arrivals, Riyuan arrivals still existed, and sales were flat, with prices falling by two or three jiao again.

Fujian Gang Smoothly Purchases Red Rough Rice

Yesterday, the Ke Xian market had good digestion, but the arrival of goods continued to be strong, and the owners were seeking to sell, so the market fell. Yesterday, the Fujian Provincial City Gang had a very good intake, purchasing 2,675 bags of mixed Xiang Red Rough Rice, with prices ranging from 7.3 yuan, 7.256 yuan to 7.2 yuan. The street's taste was also fragrant, purchasing 320 bags of Hunan Machine Red Rice, with prices ranging from 8.6 yuan to 8.55 yuan. In addition, 150 bags of Jiangxi Machine Early, with prices ranging from 8.25 yuan to 8.15 yuan, and 210 bags of Machine Late, with prices ranging from 8.92 yuan to 8.65 yuan. The high grades of each rice were stable, and the middle grades were slightly lower by four or five points due to the owners' eagerness to sell. The arrival of the rear was still strong, and the situation was not stable.

Flour and Wheat Market Slightly Different

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, foreign wheat was reported to be down by one or two jiao, and people's hearts were calm and soft, and they tended to wait and see. The factories also had the intention to sell, but because the intake was not strong, they did not dare to sell. Then, the Tianjin gang collected near-month prices in the market, and the taste was very lively. However, scattered factories still sold, and the market was not very bullish, but the trading of far-month prices was very light. In the afternoon, each round was very short, and the closing price was February at 0.25 yuan, March at 0.75 yuan, April at 0.25 yuan, May at 0.25 yuan, June was unchanged, and July was 0.25 yuan.

The foreign news of the wheat market reported a slight decrease of one or two jiao, but after the opening, the shorts covered the near-term prices strongly, so the opening price for this month was up by two fen. Then, traders resold the foreign wheat they had bought earlier in the market in the far months, and July suddenly decreased by five fen. Therefore, after the opening in the afternoon, the near months were also slightly lowered. However, the traders stopped selling when they saw that the market price was slightly lower, so July recovered by three fen. In the end, only July was slightly lower by two fen at the close, and the prices of the other months were unchanged.

Yellow Soybeans Sell Better

Green Beans Still Only The Guangdong Gang Has A Taste

Yellow soybean sales were slightly higher yesterday, and the Xiamen gang also had an intake. Zhengyang beans were two cars, and Dalian beans were purchased by the street for two cars. In addition, four or five cars of train beans were purchased by the factories. Pudong Du Beans were purchased by the Guangdong gang on the street for more than 600 bags. Although the market transaction was active, it was still dull because the purchase was high. The green bean market was still soft, and the sales relied only on the Guangdong gang. Other gangs only had two or three hundred bags, so the market was difficult to improve. Due to the lack of arrivals, the spot wheat was stable. The oil market has not opened, and the soybean cake market needs to look at the small side.

Chicago Wheat Continued to Weaken

Chicago wheat on Thursday first rose due to bad weather, and then fell due to longs taking profits. Also, 20 million bushels were traded on the 8th.

Sugar Market

Sugar Market Sales Sluggish

Yesterday, the sugar market, with the standard gold rising back to 800 taels, should have been trending well. However, the sales market has been quiet for days, and the street gangs in the Yangtze River and other places have expressed dissatisfaction with the new scale's discount issue, which has not yet been properly resolved, so transactions are even rarer. The association's price for the 24 group of white sand was called up by five points, to 15 taels and 7 qian, with no transactions. However, the industry sold hundreds of bags of Lu goods at a price of 15 taels 6 qian and 2.5 fen, which was lower than the previous market. If there are no unexpected changes in the future, there is likely to be a loosening trend. There was no change in No. 20 medium sand white and Nos. 8 and 9 Dutch red. Only 20 boxes of standard Five Blessings white ice were opened, with each price being 13 taels.

Metals

New Lead Wire Has A Sharp Increase Phenomenon

Yesterday's metal trading was still lively. The street customers were interwoven and collected, and the factory building gangs also inquired a lot, so the amount of transactions in each was considerable. Due to the rise in overseas markets, prices have an upward trend. However, the situation of the new wire is even better. The local inventory is thin, and overseas prices are rising fiercely. For example, the price from the 16th to the 20th is to be 17 pounds 2 shillings and 6 pence, and the price from the 21st to the 25th is to be 22 pounds 17 shillings and 6 pence, which is higher than the local Shanghai market. For this reason, the local industry is keen on this, so they are all receiving the current quantity. Therefore, in today's market, the upward trend of one is unique. The estimated plate is rising steadily. It is estimated that the price from the 16th to the 20th is 12 taels and 7.5 qian, and the price from the 21st to the 25th is 19 taels and 2.5 qian. The coarse color is about 10 taels. A total of one thousand and several hundred bundles were opened yesterday, and it was found that the Changjiang gang purchased them.

Free Talk

Tramps

— Zhou Lengjia

We deceive neither Heaven nor Earth, we are all 'Three Lights' guys.

What kind of 'Three Lights'? Eat it all! Use it all! Pawn it all!

Our ways of making a living are: begging, gambling on the ground, overturning coffins, pretending to have accurate aim, shaking the road, pushing rickshaws across bridges.

Today, we are lucky! Early in the morning, as soon as I went out for a stroll, I struck it rich, I bumped into a young man in a Western suit, with a girl of eighteen or nineteen clinging to his arm. That girl was wearing a leather coat, and a large section of a blood-red cheongsam was exposed below the coat, with a pair of high heels, clicking with each step, really flashy! Damn! The weather is so cold, and my worn-out clothes have several holes, the cold wind whistling and trying to get into the holes, making my whole body shiver and feel uncomfortable. This kid, he's having a good time, the couple squeezing together tightly, their eyes seeming to grow on their foreheads, not glancing at anyone else at all. I glanced at this kid, and I felt very uncomfortable in my heart, intending to provoke him, to argue with him. They went east, and I stuck to them going east, they went west, and I stuck to them going west. Believe it or not, I guessed that this couple must have been so lovey-dovey that they were confused, and as I stuck to them like that, they gave me a coin on the left, and a coin on the right, giving me a large pile. Finally, this kid realized what was going on, stomped his foot, and shouted at me:

"What are you doing? Get lost!"

I shrugged my shoulders, spat, and muttered: "It's cheap for you, you little bastard, I'm not going to cut the tops off your boots." Then I walked away.

My stomach is also acting up! Without money, it's silent, but as soon as it's near money, it growls and rumbles non-stop. I was just thinking of buying two fried dumplings to eat with the money from that tall Shandong man's pancake stall, but for some reason, suddenly, "Achoo! Achoo!" two sneezes came one after another, and tears and snot came in a large stream with yawns. Oh! Good heavens! My opium addiction is acting up! I couldn't care less about being hungry, I quickly ran to a small sundries store near Chaoyangmen in a few strides, bought a few opium pellets, two or three pieces of dirt skin, and hastily swallowed them, which barely satisfied my addiction. But, as a result, all the money I had just begged for was gone!

What to do? I have to think of a way! This stomach keeps causing me trouble, taking care of the dark rice, and the white rice is left empty, there are always times when a hunchback falls, and neither side is solid. I squatted at the sundries store near Chaoyangmen, my mind running through a lot of ideas, but none of them were feasible. The weather is so cold, and it's early in the morning, there are only a few ghost-like figures on the road, where can I go to do business? If only I could be like those tough older brothers, with a spray gun in my hand, then I wouldn't be afraid of not making a profit; but I don't have that equipment, I can't even do the early morning rounds, let alone forceful robberies! I had no choice but to rub my stomach, tighten my belt, and gather my strength to rush forward. (To be continued)

Two Kinds of "Incoherent"

— He Jiaqian

When people criticize articles, those of the type of Chinese language teachers mostly focus on "coherence" or "incoherence." However, writing Chinese well is actually very difficult to be "coherent." Even masters like Sima Qian, the Grand Historian, if you examine his articles carefully, no matter from the perspective of vocabulary, grammar, or rhetoric, you can find places that are "incoherent."

But I'm not talking about these now. What I want to say is that within the general term "incoherent," there are several kinds based on the reasons. Generally speaking, there are cases where the author's logic has not yet been cleared, and there are also cases where it could actually be coherent, but due to various relationships, the author does not dare to be coherent, or is unwilling to be coherent.

For example, the October 31st record in "×× Newspaper" about the "Jiangdu Tax Resistance Uprising," under the clever title of "Villagers Stir Up Trouble for the Second Time," the account of Chen Youliang's death states:

"Chen Youliang saw Liu Jinfa, who carried a pistol, among the official soldiers and police, and actually wanted to snatch Liu's pistol. He was shot and killed when a bullet was discharged from the chamber. The police also fired a volley of blank shots, and the villagers began to retreat."

The phrase "official" need not be added before "soldiers and police"—that's unnecessary. But I won't discuss that here. The strangest thing is that the bullet is written about as if it were a living thing, able to run out of the chamber on its own. But this makes the "also" in the following sentence incoherent. It would be more appropriate to change the previous sentence to "He was shot to death." If you want to preserve the previous sentence, then change the last two sentences to "The police also fired blank shots at the same time, and the villagers began to retreat." Only then would it be perfectly balanced, and have nothing to do with the soldiers and police, although the logic is still a bit strange.

Such strange articles often appear now. Actually, it's not that the authors are incapable of being coherent, but rather that they are afraid of not being allowed to be coherent, so they don't dare to be coherent from the start. The most intelligent people don't talk about these things, and become "art for art's sake" artists. The second most intelligent people use various methods to embellish this incoherence, and become "nationalist" writers. But both belong to the category of being "unwilling to be coherent."

The Aims of the "International Women's Association"

— Jian Feng

In the past, when people praised a woman, they would often say things like "beauty that can be eaten" or "enough to topple cities and states." The meaning of these adjectives, to put it plainly, is that women are merely objects for men to play with. In recent years, women have gradually awakened. They believe that in addition to their responsibilities in the family, women should also contribute to human society. Therefore, they are working to improve women's knowledge on the one hand, and engaging in the women's suffrage movement on the other. To unify the women's movement, they also have the organization of the International Women's Association. "Give me back my freedom, give me back my equality" is the cry of the association.

The International Woman Suffrage Alliance has been established for a long time, and last year marked the date of its twelfth congress. The association originally planned to hold the congress in Athens, the capital of Greece, in May last year, but because it was the height of the world economic panic, a large sum of money was needed to convene the congress, and the travel expenses for sending representatives from all over the world were also difficult to raise. After a meeting of the executive committee, it was decided to postpone the temporary congress to this spring in Marseille. Invitations have now been sent out to women's organizations from various countries that participate in the association, inviting them to send representatives to attend. It is said that Japan is also on the list of invitees.

The main purpose of this temporary congress is that in recent years, the world economy has fallen into a state of great panic, and the occupations, positions, etc. that women have gained through years of struggle have all been affected by it, and now most of them are being taken away by men again. In addition, countries such as Greece, France, Bulgaria, Belgium, Romania, Switzerland, etc. still only recognize women's citizenship, but refuse to give them suffrage. In addition, countries in Asia and a large part of South America have not yet resolved the issue of women's suffrage. Even in countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany, where women's suffrage has already been implemented, women are still subject to differential treatment under the law. All these things are considered extremely unfair by members of the International Women's Association. These are the issues that the association wants to discuss and resolve. In addition, the abolition of prostitution and the abolition of slave ownership and concubinage in African and Eastern countries will also be put forward for discussion at the congress.

The association strongly supports world peace. The members of the association all have great ideals, aiming to work with men to eliminate future wars and solve the world economic panic. The association once declared: "We are an organization that advocates that men and women should enjoy equal treatment in politics, economy, law, and morality. We will use political means and methods to achieve our goals. We do not want to see the cruel wars of mutual slaughter appear in the world again. We pray that human peace will last forever. The League of Nations is an international parliament, it is the messenger of maintaining world peace, and it is what our women have always supported. We hope that it can uphold justice and help us achieve our demands. We hope to work with men to realize the world's eternal peace and seek the revival of the world economy. This is our mission, and we are moving in this direction! ·····"

But world peace has already been completely destroyed by Japan, and the comedy stage of the League of Nations has been overturned by Japan with one foot. I wonder what kind of supernatural powers these "well-meaning" female bodhisattvas will have when they meet this spring to subdue the beastly Japanese?

Welcoming the Lanterns

— Wen Bing

Qi'er, squatting under the steps, was wearing a tattered, lined short jacket and a pair of gray open-crotch pants; his left hand was clutching a water chestnut that a vendor had dropped on the ground, but half of it had already gone into his stomach; his right hand was holding a stone, "drawing symbols" on the bluestone slab; two strings of yellow noodles-like snot hung from his nose, neatly hanging under his nostrils, waiting for him to start eating the remaining half of the water chestnut, and these "yellow noodles" would also go in with it.

He suddenly froze, his eyes staring unblinkingly at a hole in the wall. The scene of carrying lanterns during the Lantern Festival last night was playing out before his eyes.

"Hidden Dragon, Hidden Dragon, Hidden..." Some older children, holding a lion lantern filled with candlelight, rushed straight onto the street, banging gongs and drums.

"Tang tang..." Other children, who were a bit younger, banged on small gongs and drums, holding a white rabbit lantern, and rushed after the lion lantern.

"Heh! Heh! ... Heh!" This group was all seven- or eight-year-old children wearing dazzling clothes, each holding a bamboo pole, topped with rabbit, bird, or butterfly lanterns, shouting back and forth on the short street. Little Qi'er was first surprised and dazed, then his eyes turned red. He went to ask his mother with a hopeful heart. But in the end, he could only shed two lines of hot tears, and open his small mouth to "blow the trumpet."

Suddenly, he moved his gaze from the hole in the wall to the doorway of his house, quickly straightened his small legs, and used his hand to pull up the pants that were about to fall down; wiped the "yellow noodles" with his sleeve; his lips slightly parted and smiled; he quickly threw away the stone in his hand, took small steps, and ran home.

Not long after, he was holding a thin bamboo pole in his hand, with his father's old straw shoe, covered in mud, hanging high on the pole.

"Heh! Welcoming the lanterns! Heh! Welcoming the lanterns!" He looked up at the sky, looked at his "straw shoe lantern," grinned, and cheered non-stop; even though the mud and sand on the bottom of the straw shoe, like pepper, were falling into his small mouth, he didn't care.

Random Thoughts from Qu Lu

— Yu Zhan

1. Sichuanese and Opium

A friend who had returned after retiring from Chengdu University said that Sichuan had a lot of opium, and the special tax was a major source of government revenue. He also said that local people who had some power always carried two guns with them, a long gun for killing others and a short gun for killing themselves. His words were full of sighs. I said, the people of Sichuan have been planting opium for at least a thousand years. The guest asked me what my basis was. I said, the late Tang Dynasty poet Yong Tao's poem "Westward Return to Xiegu" says: "Passing through the dangerous plank road and coming out of Bao Xie, I have gone through the plain and seem to have arrived home. Endless sorrow of travelers is scattered today, and the mianang flower is seen for the first time in front of the horse." Mianang flower is the poppy flower. Su Shi has a poem: "The Taoist advises to drink chicken su water, and the boy can decoct poppy soup." Su Zhe also has a poem about planting medicinal seedlings, singing about the poppy. It can be seen that people in the Tang and Song Dynasties regarded opium as a precious medicine for treating diseases. Yong Tao and Su were both from Shu (Sichuan), so it can be seen that the people of Sichuan had a relationship with opium as early as the Tang and Song Dynasties.

2. Lotus Drop Poet

My friend Zhigang Liwu loves to listen to Lotus Drop the most. Liwu can also snap his fingers and compose poems on the spot, like singing Lotus Drop, which his friends use as a joke.

For the past five or six years, we have all made a living by running around, drifting in all directions, and the Lotus Drop of Changsha is no longer heard. After the September 18th Incident, I saw the Tan Hui of the Bubu Ting Cao Zhai published in Shen Bao, which often contained vernacular poems lamenting current events, which had the rhyme of Lotus Drop. I also secretly took the verses of the Tang Dynasty poet Zhang Hu, "Casually collect words and phrases, boast to the people and call them begging," and wrote dozens of poems such as "National Affairs Yin" to express my sorrow and anger. Composing wildly according to events is no different from the meaning of Lotus Drop, but I have never used it to beg for money to exchange for rice. I don't know when Lotus Drop started. In Yuan zaju and Ming legends, beggars are seen singing Lotus Drop. Wu Deng Hui Yuan recorded that Yu Daopo followed the crowd to visit Langya. One day, he heard a beggar singing Lotus Drop and had a great enlightenment. It seems that Lotus Drop already existed in the Song Dynasty. Also, Quan Tang Shi quoted Hou Qinglu: "There was a zheshan (folded shirt) zuizi in the Tang Dynasty, who danced and sang, 'Holding the board and singing wildly to beg for money, drifting in the river and following fate, straight until old, always like this, better than playing power in dangerous times.'" Could this be the earliest Lotus Drop poet?

Long Form Fiction

Divergent Paths of Love and the Times (Draft)

— Zhang Maiping

Thinking this, he could no longer restrain himself. He strode straight into Mrs. Tsuruko's room.

"You're bullying Mr. Zeng while he's not home!"

In his excitement, he was still able to consider this justification, and declare war on that Japanese fellow. That Japanese fellow was just about to get up and give him a morning greeting, but unexpectedly, he got a slap on the corner of his mouth.

"Aha! Aha!"

Haiquan shouted, and the second slap flew over. This time, the slap really angered the Japanese fellow. He retreated to the edge of the futon and took off his Chinese robe, threw it on the ground, and began to rub his fists and wipe his palms, preparing for "Sumo."

"Terrible!..."

Haiquan heard a sharp voice like a pen tip coming from behind. At the moment of difficulty, he thought of retreating, fearing being looked down upon by the Japanese fellow; not retreating, and fighting the Japanese fellow, no matter who won or lost, he would definitely suffer. He was afraid that he would be locked up in the police station for a few days! A few days would be okay, but what if he was sentenced to a fairly long prison term? Because the laws in the concession protected the imperialists from trampling on Chinese civilians!

"Mr. Lin, he's my father!"

He was embraced by her, and at the same time, he smelled an intoxicating fragrance. While he was thinking about what attitude to take to deal with the current predicament, he was desperately appreciating the fragrance emanating from her.

She spoke to the Japanese fellow again in Japanese. He had not yet understood what attitude the Japanese fellow was expressing, and he had already been dragged and half-hugged by Mrs. Tsuruko with all her might, and pulled out of the room.

His face was pale, and he couldn't say a word.

"Mr. Lin, I'm sorry. I should have told you earlier that he's my father... Go back to your room, for my sake."
